The room was very quiet. There were not many people in the hotel and there were no groups. I haven't met anyone in the corridor these few days I've been here. Most are business people and independent tourists.
Facilities and hygiene: It smells good when you enter the hotel, the room facilities are new, and the bedding is clean and tidy. The shower room and toilet are separated by a wall. Can be used at the same time without embarrassment. The bathroom is large and has a table to sit on. The water is strong and the temperature is stable. The bathtub is big and wide, making it very comfortable to take a bath.
Service: As soon as the order was confirmed, the dedicated butler Vivian called and added WeChat. Come and ask about arrival time and any requirements. I asked to reserve a room with an unobstructed river view for me, and Vivian indeed reserved a room with an unrivaled river view for me. She also sent a greeting message after arriving at the store, asking me to contact her if I had any questions or needs. Makes me feel like service is all around me. I also requested a late check-out and was given a free late check-out. Check-in at the front desk was also very fast. When the service staff saw people queuing up, they immediately opened a counter to quickly check in for the queuing guests. The hotel lobby is on the 69th floor. To go to your room and to the first floor, you have to switch to the elevator in the lobby. At first, I was worried that the wait would take too long and that it would be too troublesome. There is actually no need to worry. First, I took a look at the hotels in Chongqing. Most of the high-rise buildings have to use elevators. Second: The service of the concierge is simply not that good. There is the hotel‚Äôs concierge counter on the first floor. Every time I see a guest coming, I run over and press the elevator first. There are two elevators on the first floor that lead directly to the hotel. Don‚Äôt mix them with others. , the elevator came soon. When we arrived at the lobby, the concierge service staff saw a guest coming, and immediately ran to press the elevator for the guest to go to the room. This elevator is also exclusive to the hotel, so you basically don‚Äôt have to wait. I didn't find this troublesome or long waiting time at all. There was a concierge, I didn't see his name clearly, he was tall, and he smiled when he saw the guests opening the elevator door far away. His smile was particularly enthusiastic, sincere, and full of joy. As soon as I see him smile, I want to laugh too. It makes people feel happy and kind.
Others: There is a coffee machine in the room, four bottles of mineral water (daily), three coffee capsules, and 6 TWG tea bags for free. The thoughtful thing is that there are also two disposable coffee cups. You can brew coffee and drink it while walking.
The only thing I would like to suggest is that there are no rubber slippers for bathing. You have to wear disposable cotton mops to take a shower. Although the cotton mops are of good quality and thick, they are difficult to dry when wet. But you can ask for two pairs to change into dry ones after bathing.
The hotel does not take the initiative to provide disposable items, but you can call the room to request them, which is very comprehensive. Everything you want is available. There is a list in the bathroom.
The price is a little more expensive than others, but the location is good, the setting is new, the scenery is beautiful, and there are not many people. I didn't book a room with breakfast, so I won't comment.

The deluxe room is very spacious, our room is facing the Jiefangbei, and the view and landscape are great. The large floor-to-ceiling windows provide good light during the day, and the lights at night are even more gorgeous. The beds were comfortable and the bathtub was huge. The room is equipped with a capsule coffee machine, and you can drink hot coffee every day. I had a good time with my friends.

All in all a great stay experience.
